Verdict in the Farmer's Wife-Killing Case 142

Chen Qinquan, a farmer from Zhigangfen, near Tailai Bridge, outside the south gate of this county, returned home from work at about 5:00 pm on the 21st of last month. Because his wife, Li, lost one yuan of association money, a quarrel arose. Chen, in a fit of rage, killed his wife with a kitchen knife. The case has been tried several times, and it was originally intended to be sentenced to death. Fortunately, Chen's mother-in-law repeatedly pleaded for leniency, so he was sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment with shackles on the 8th of this month.

[News of the Relocation of the Public Education Center

The Public Education Center of Baijijiang, in the eighth district of the county, has been officially established since April of the 18th year and has been in operation for a year and a half. There have already been seven projects: public schools, public libraries, public entertainment venues, public lecture halls, public reading materials, public sports fields, and public tea gardens. In the next semester, there will be organizations such as public hospitals and cooperatives. Recently, the center suddenly received an order from the Education Bureau to move to Chonggu Town in the ninth district in the next semester. All the staff were stunned after seeing the order. In order to facilitate the progress of various projects in the next semester, the center submitted a statement of reasons to the Education Department requesting exemption from relocation and requesting permission to continue operating in order to save trouble and maintain existing achievements.

Chuansha

Aftermath of the Flood in Hengsha 143

More than 16,000 mu of farmland in the dikes and ponds of the sixth district (Hengsha) of the county were washed away by the tides, more than 100 houses collapsed, and more than 2,000 households were affected. The county government, in addition to sending personnel to the disaster area for investigation, also convened a meeting at 1:00 pm on the 7th with local charitable organizations and gentry to discuss disaster relief measures. The meeting was chaired by County Magistrate Ruan and resolved: (1) To organize a disaster relief committee to handle all disaster relief matters. (2) The committee members will be appointed by the county government through letters to Lu Zhuping, Tao Qing, Lu Wenmei, and 22 others. (3) Zhiyuan Shantang, the county chamber of commerce, and the sixth district office will first send personnel to conduct an on-site investigation of the disaster situation and report to the committee for further action. (4) The dike project will be the responsibility of the sixth district office to supervise the completion of the project by all business owners within a time limit.

Fengxian

Kidnappers Executed by Firing Squad 144

Liu Boxian, a local resident, also known as Fang Bokang, a major criminal in the Lu Zihe kidnapping case in Fang Sixteen Tu near Zhuangxing, was sentenced to death by the county judicial trial in accordance with the regulations for punishing bandits. Yesterday afternoon, under the verification of County Magistrate Shen, Secretary Yang Shudu and Squadron Leader Ding Zhiyan were appointed to escort him to the Dongshi Baijia Ancestral Hall for execution by firing squad. It is said that there is still one suspect, Tang Sicheng, who is currently under investigation.

Bandit Intimidation at Jinhui and Qixian Bridges 145

The 8-year-old son of a Chen family in Jinhui Bridge Township in the sixth district of the county was kidnapped by bandits the night before last and a huge ransom was demanded. At the same time, in Qixian Bridge Town, seven miles away, all merchants and residents have been receiving threatening letters from bandits demanding loans of several thousand or hundreds of yuan for several days. Inspector Chen Jin was dispatched to investigate and arrest the bandits in order to solve the case.

A Martyr Killed Herself to Show Her Integrity 146

Xu Wang, a rural woman who opened a fish stall in Dongshi, Zhuangxing, and her husband, Geng Jia, worked as a hired hand in Shanghai, but his income was not enough.

Page 10

She and her mother ran the business themselves to support the family and were known for their thrift and virtue. However, recently, rumors spread in the neighborhood that the woman had an affair with Shao Xiang, who lived with her. The woman, who had been falsely accused, could not defend herself and was filled with injustice. She committed suicide by inhaling smoke the day before yesterday to prove her integrity.

Wujiaqiao Receives Threatening Letters 147

In the past two months, all those with slight assets in Wujiaqiao Town have received bandit letters demanding loans of three to four hundred yuan. It is said that at the time, because they did not dare to expect punishment, most of them prepared the money and paid it in order to avoid trouble. However, the town suddenly received a threatening letter from the Shanghai Post Office the day before yesterday, stating that it had been reported that the First Army of Taihu would come to the town to loot within ten days and would be detrimental to certain families. The letter said that the army knew that the merchants in the town were quite righteous and could not bear to sit idly by, so it was specially sent to inform them to prepare in advance and that certain families should leave quickly to avoid harm. The people in the town were panicked upon receiving this news, and some even moved their entire families to avoid it. In order to maintain order, the town office decided to immediately implement special martial law and specially sent Wang Daoming to the county today to request the stationing of troops to assist in maintaining order.

Bandits Rob Weapons in Gaoqiao 148

Gaoqiao Town, two miles away from Fengcheng, was suddenly attacked by more than twenty bandits wearing miscellaneous yellow and gray uniforms the night before last. They surrounded the town's public security police station and robbed a quick gun and a set of uniforms. They then went to the salt police patrol boat No. 2 and confiscated two Mauser rifles and many bullets. Before leaving, they went to the Chen family's house, broke down the door, and robbed everything before leaving with shouts.

Ji Case: Guarantee to Hand Over the Ungrateful Son 149

In the case of Ji Ahe in the 32nd Tu of Malu Township being beaten with an axe by his eldest son Ji Yinlong, the county government has repeatedly issued warrants for his arrest, but the ungrateful son has not yet been captured. Now, the township chief Wang Chaofu has learned that the ungrateful son is still in the house of the Tu chief Wang Mu, so he specially wrote to the district office to report to the county for arrest. At the same time, Ji Ahe, who returned home after receiving medical treatment in Shanghai, also reported the previous situation. After the county verified the facts, it sent police officers yesterday to summon the Tu chief and order him to hand over the ungrateful son within three days for punishment.

Suzhou

Forced Removal of Shops in Guanqian 150

Wei Zumo, director of the Wuxian Construction Bureau, in order to renovate Guanqian Street and expand the street area, ordered the shops in Guanqian to move and rebuild by July 15 and complete the work by September 15. Therefore, the road surface and ditches have been excavated. However, although the shops on both sides of Zhengshanmen have been vacated, the merchants of each shop intend to rebuild the houses there into three-story buildings to increase the view. However, the county government decided in a meeting that only flat houses would be allowed to be built. Therefore, the merchants have been holding a wait-and-see attitude and have not hired workers to demolish the buildings. Wei Zumo, director of the Construction Bureau, was deeply concerned that the shops were delaying and that the deadline would be exceeded. Therefore, yesterday, he specially hired a large number of Jiangbei workers to forcibly demolish the buildings and ordered the landlords to build them within a time limit.

Interruption of Rice Price Stabilization Program is Feared 151

The price stabilization bureaus in the city and suburbs have been notified by the Sales Storage Committee that there are only two periods worth of rice left in storage. The directors of each bureau immediately telegraphed the county government to find a way to maintain the program to help the people, as the county government originally set the period at three months and it has not yet been two months. County Magistrate Huang therefore scheduled a meeting for the morning of the 12th to convene members of the price stabilization committee and local people to discuss solutions.

Personnel Sent to Investigate the Chuansha Prison Break 152

On the night of the previous day, a convicted bandit, Wu Yaoliang, escaped from Chuansha County Prison late at night. Zheng Ligeng, the prison warden of the county, reported the incident to the Higher Court the previous day. After receiving the report, Chief Judge Lin specially sent Yao Guozhang, director of the prison section, to investigate yesterday (9th).

List of Names of Those Who Escaped Danger 153

Since the bandit leader of Taihu was defeated by Commander Qi Guoliang's team on the 4th of this month, all the bandits have dispersed. In addition to Captain Wang Wusheng and Zheng Xin, a member of the Dongshan Defense Corps, who escaped danger on the same day, the following people escaped danger the previous day: Inspector Huang Wangmin, Pu Minghua, the accountant of the Dalu Small Ferry, Yu Bokang, the accountant of the Feihu Small Ferry, passengers Zhu Rongsheng, Zhou Zhaoqi, Zhou Fan, Xi Yichun, Qian Ziqin, Ge Shousheng, Song Yu, Li Xu, Yang Wanlun, Wang Asheng, Yang Han, and his 14-year-old son, for a total of sixteen people. Those who have not escaped danger include Shen Guisun, Shen Ernan, Shen Wunan, his maid, Shi Jieshan, Jin Yunshi, Zhu Hongsheng, Zhu Tao, Li Rengen, Xia Lianfu, Jin Zhongshu, Xu Bingkun, and Shi Zishan, for a total of thirteen people.

Complications Arise from Purchasing Kerosene 154

The Deshiji Kerosene Company on Hengma Road outside Guanmen purchased 600 boxes of Happiness brand kerosene from the Shanghai head office last month, worth about 5,000 yuan. Hai Gu, a ship bureau, hired the shipowner Wu Fuyuan to transport it to Suzhou on the 26th of last month. The local branch has not seen it arrive for many days, so it sent a letter to the ship bureau for inquiries. The bureau found that Wu's ship had not returned to Shanghai. After investigation, it was learned that Wu had a shipmate named Ji who was in Wuxi. Therefore, on the 6th of this month, they sent someone to report to the Wuxi County Police Team, who arrested Ji. Ji confessed that after the ship arrived at the Damaji Bridge outside Loumen, Suzhou on the 2nd of this month, Wu Fuyuan brought people to the ship the next day and transported 200 boxes of goods away. On the third day, they transported the remaining 400 boxes completely. Yesterday, Xie Fengtai learned the news and found that Xiangxing Leji, located at No. 2 Taohuawu, had purchased the stolen goods. Therefore, he reported the information to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, and Patrol Officer Xu Boying went to arrest Shi Jinquan, the manager of the store. Shi Jinquan confessed that Zhang Jiantang (also known as Zhang Bin, the owner of the Minsheng Firecracker Factory) from outside the Gate of the Gods introduced him to buy the kerosene. There were a total of 573 boxes, 100 boxes were sold to Dalongsheng Rice Shop on Heyan Street, 100 boxes were sold to Tongfu outside Loumen, and he bought 350 boxes for himself, each box costing 5 yuan and 6 jiao. There were also 23 boxes that Zhang Jiantang bought himself. He took three boxes home for use and stored the remaining boxes in his shop. As a result, Patrol Officer Xu and the detective team arrested Zhang Jiantang outside Nantongzimen, brought him to the bureau, and also arrested Wu Fuyuan for questioning.

Disguised Negotiation to Redeem Tickets and Open Fire with Bandits 155

The First Squadron of the 14th Water Police Team and the Second Squadron of the Guerrilla Team searched for the remnants of the bandits in the area of Laotaimiao in Miaoqian Xigang. The gunboats were stopped near the temple, and small fishing boats were hired in disguise to investigate Laotaimiao. Two plainclothes police officers were sent to disguise themselves as redemption negotiators of the kidnapped victims in Dongshan and patrol back and forth. At 11:00 pm on the 8th, several bandits disguised as farmers came to negotiate the redemption of the tickets. They asked what kind of boat the small fishing boat was. The water police replied that it was the one who came to receive the redemption tickets. The bandits said that it was not right and opened fire. The two plainclothes police officers also opened fire with their box cannons. The main force of the gunboats immediately advanced and opened fire for one hour. Four Taihu bandits were killed on the spot, a box cannon and dozens of rounds of ammunition were seized, and the head of the small bandit leader of Taihu was taken down and hung in front of the temple for public display. Currently, the remnants of the Taihu bandits are divided into two groups: Zhong Zhaokui and Zhou A'si and Wang Zhongyi, who are still hiding in the reeds of Yangcheng Lake.

Wuxi

Change of Director of the Epidemic Hospital 156

Since its opening, the Yanshou Sidian Epidemic Hospital outside Dongmen has benefited the general public. Sun Zuji, the county magistrate of this county and the director of the hospital, recently submitted his resignation to the provincial government. It is said that he will also firmly resign from the position of director of the epidemic hospital and intends to invite Jiang Daoshan to succeed him.

River-Sedimented Bandits of Jiangyin Escorted Back to Face Trial 157

The Eighth Branch of the Xiyi Public Security Bureau previously apprehended seven bandits, namely Zhang Xuetang, Wang Baochuan, Chen A'da, Huang Dabao, Wang A'er, Sun Guanshi, and Gong Zhangshi, along with a suspect named Miao Xianglin, at the Huishang Inn outside the North Gate of Tantou Lane in Xiyi. They also seized seven homemade bombs and a quantity of stolen goods, which were all escorted to the county for interrogation. It has now been learned that the captured criminals often used aliases and committed multiple crimes in Jiangyin. For example, Zhang Xuetang's real name is Gong Baogen, Wang Baochuan's real name is Zhang A'ba, Chen A'da's real name is Zhang Fuqing, Huang Dabao's real name is Zhang Enbao, and Wang A'er's real name is Zhang A'er. All are long-time bandits in Jiangyin who have used aliases. Gong Chenshi is Gong Baogen's wife. Furthermore, Gong Baogen sent a letter to Zhu Dabao, a resident of Gongjiatan in Jiangyin County, on July 16th, demanding 2,000 silver dollars under threat. Recently, the Jiangyin authorities learned that Gong and his accomplices had been arrested in Xiyi. Yesterday, they dispatched Zhu, the head of the Fifth Jia Protective Corps of the Fourteenth District of Jiangyin County, to Xiyi by boat to identify the bandits. Confirming that they were indeed the river-sedimented bandits of Jiangyin, the county government prepared a document ordering the police to escort the bandits back to Jiangyin for legal proceedings.

Clues to the Sun Lane Robbery Case 158

The Sun family of Sun Leikui (also known as Jin Kui) in Sun Lane, Yinqiao Township, the Sixteenth District of Xiyi (i.e., Wan'an City), was robbed and the head of the household was injured the other night. In addition to robbing silver dollars and land deeds, the bandits burned all the IOUs. Furthermore, on the morning of the robbery, Sun Leikui's son, Deqing (an acupuncturist), had treated someone for a fright at Yu Fulin's house. Therefore, when the bandits entered the Sun family's home, they impersonated Fulin, falsely claiming to be there for medical assistance. When the bandits left, they said that if Sun wanted the land deeds back, he could entrust Yang Peicheng to bring money to redeem them. However, Yang Peicheng used to be a teacher in the Sun family and is known to be upright, thus making it a clear attempt to frame him. Judging from the bandits' burning of IOUs and their words, they must be familiar with the family. The clues are plentiful, and it should not be difficult to solve the case. Currently, both the Yang and Yu families, as well as local gentry, have issued statements to avoid being implicated. Sun Leikui came to the city the day before yesterday to report the injuries to the county and request the arrest of the bandits.

Joint Military, Police, and National Defense Meeting 159

The Wuyi Military, Police, and Regiment Joint Defense Office held a meeting at the Xianbing Camp headquarters in Chongfa Temple on the 8th to discuss various defense matters: (1) It was resolved to divide the urban area into five major police duty zones, jointly responsible for defense by the Xianbing Camp, Public Security Bureau, Police Force, Business Regiment, and the First Branch. (2) It was resolved to assign teams to guard each city gate, install telephones, and the opening and closing of the city gates would be commanded by the Joint Defense Office. (3) It was resolved that the water area would be guarded by the Water Police Team's Tenth Squad, which would dispatch patrol boats for patrol. (4) It was resolved that the Joint Defense Office should set up secret agents and requested that the Water Police Team Leader Han Yunbo come to the office for consultation.

Jiangyin

Disruptive Offender Executed by Order 161

Zhou Busheng (also known as Pusheng), a thug who disturbed the peace, robbed weapons, and injured a squad leader of the Xianbing in Beiwai on the 4th, was arrested along with others. After investigating the severity of their crimes, it was found that Zhou was the main culprit, and after reporting to higher authorities, the headquarters ordered Commander Yang to punish him according to the law. He was executed by firing squad at 4:00 PM on the 8th. Cao A'wu, Zhu Shisheng, and Yao Yucheng were sentenced according to Article 72, Section 1, Item 2 of the Army, Navy, and Air Force Criminal Law for instigating others to cause disturbances: Cao A'wu to three years of imprisonment, Zhu Shisheng to five years, and Yao Yucheng to two years. For those with lighter offenses, Xian Biao and An Ziming were each punished with 100 military baton strikes, and Sun Zongyan, Tang Libin, Meng Yunfa, Li Xue, Wang Deqing, Zhang Rongting, and Yuan Guanghai were each punished with 50 military baton strikes. Ye Desheng and Qian Songlin were each punished with 150 military baton strikes, and Yin Xiangyun, Xue Lifa, Li Songlin, and Zheng Baode were each punished with 20 military baton strikes. All were returned to custody, and the handling of the matter was telegraphed to higher authorities for review.

Gunned Down Male Corpse Found at Yangshu Bridge 163

Yesterday morning, an unidentified male corpse with gunshot wounds was discovered under Yangshu Bridge in Dongwai. He appeared to be a government official, wearing black Xiangyun gauze pants. He was about twenty years old, and the bullet entered from his back. He had a cloth-made box gun pouch on his body. The town head of the area reported the case to the county for examination.

Eradication of Stray Dogs Not Successful 164

County Head Li Leng, based on a letter from Zhang Ya'fu stating that there were many stray dogs in the city, which were detrimental to hygiene, ordered the district office to cooperate with the Public Security Bureau to register domestic dogs and to prepare a large batch of steamed buns containing Croton tiglium and red arsenic to poison stray dogs inside and outside the city. However, because the medicine's properties were conflicting, the dogs vomited after eating them, and none were poisoned to death. The district office plans to continue poisoning the dogs at a later date.

Movement to Demolish the Construction Department's Screen Wall 165

Yesterday (the 9th) at 3:00 PM, various circles in the provincial capital held a general meeting at the county party headquarters to discuss the movement to demolish the Construction Department's screen wall. More than 50 representatives attended. The matters discussed were: (1) The meeting was named the "Provincial Movement to Demolish Illegal Construction Department Screen Walls." The proposal was passed. (2) The Construction Department's screen wall illegally occupies private land and obstructs road administration and should be completely demolished. It was resolved that: (A) Representatives from the county executive committee, the press, the chamber of commerce, and the meeting would be nominated to meet with Chairman Ye to request that the Construction Department immediately demolish the screen wall completely and not interfere with the original business of the landowners. (B) If there is no satisfactory response, the second step of the plan will be decided by the next representative assembly. (3) The proposal to set the date for the next representative assembly was decided to be convened by the county executive committee next Monday at 2:00 PM.

Under party rule, service should be given, and it is not appropriate to discuss the size of the position or to rashly come to the department seeking a position. The wording of the request is absurd and improper and should be reprimanded."

Yangzhou

Twists and Turns in the Case of Trafficking in Persons Again 167

The Public Security Bureau of this county previously uncovered a case of trafficking in persons at the Bo'ai Hospital on Zuo Wei Street. It is now learned that the First Branch of the bureau received a telegram from Tang, the section chief of the judicial section of the general bureau, ordering that the suspect Wang Buhai be quickly escorted to the general bureau for handling. After receiving the telegram, Branch Chief Chen immediately demanded the person from a lawyer who had bailed out Wang and others. However, the lawyer sent a letter to Section Chief Tang, stating that the case should be handled by the judicial authorities and that the bureau could not interfere. It is said that Tang believes that the girl, Wang Shaoqing, who was abducted by the suspect, has requested considerable protection, and even if she is sent to the court, the bureau should first submit a detailed account of the case to the court for legal punishment and cannot simply ignore the case because the person has already been released on bail. It is now said that Tang is determined to bring the suspect to justice, but it is not known how Branch Chief Chen will handle it.

Bandits Shoot Homeowner 170

The home of Wu Yongsheng, a farmer in Xiejiaxiang, the first village of the second district of the tenth district, was suddenly attacked by six or seven bandits on the night of the third of this month. Continued Account of the Shagou Town Robbery 171

Shibou Town in the tenth district of the county borders Shagou Town in Yanyi. Yesterday, there were rumors of bandits robbing the town. It is now learned that the details of the robbery involve the leader of the police team stationed in the town, who, upon seeing a civilian boat passing through the town, ordered it to stop. The boat ignored the order, and the team leader became furious and immediately opened fire, killing three people on the boat. The various agencies and the public in the town were alarmed and immediately telegraphed the Yancheng County Government. The county head appointed a new team leader to take over the town, but he was also shot and killed by a certain squad leader. Seeing that he had caused a disaster, the squad leader gathered his subordinates, defense soldiers, and nearby bandits to carry out a large-scale robbery. It is said that pawnshops and money shops suffered the greatest losses. The squad leader also took all the guns in the town and fled.

Sixian

Near News About Bandits Disturbing Sixian 180

In Qiujiagang, the southeastern village of Sixian, some bandits with guns have asked for money and guns in villages since several months ago, frequently causing disturbance. On July 28th, they gathered five or six hundred local ruffians, hooligans, beggars and bandits, and surrounded Shangtangji in the fourth district, very aggressively. However, the public officials of the district office and all the officers and soldiers of the Self-Defense Corps, using various excuses, ignored the defense. The public were in a hurry. The local militia in the market area implemented self-defense. While the fight was going on, the officers and soldiers of the self-defense corps suddenly mutinied and threw themselves into the communist party, opening fire on the militia. The militia suffered heavy casualties from internal and external attacks. The Southeast was extremely chaotic. Later, Ma Hanzhang, Zhang Wenbo and others of the second district personally led the Self-Defense Corps and the local militia to rush to aid the villagers at night, and finally repelled the bandits. It is said that they are still entrenched in the southern part of the city, gathering more and more, and their momentum is huge. The residents of the city and countryside are extremely alarmed.

Difficulties in Raising Debt 181

The Zhejiang Construction Public Debt was allocated to Pinghu this time, with an amount of 280,000 yuan. After receiving the order, County Head Fang Li convened a meeting of wealthy people in the county, but due to the famine years, there were no concrete results. After several meetings, only a few people attended, and there was no real progress. County Head Fang, due to his responsibilities, reported the difficulties in raising funds to the province and also ran to Beijing and Shanghai to solicit donations from fellow villagers abroad. He repeatedly tried to arrange for the allocation of the Zhao Highway Public Debt (according to the highway public debt, Pingyi was allocated 100,000 yuan). While the matter was in progress, Chairman Zhang of this province sent separate letters to various wealthy households, designating allocations, totaling 486,000 yuan. The original quota for the general wealthy households was already difficult to allocate, but now it has exceeded more than half, which is unbearable. Therefore, they have jointly stated their difficulty in meeting the quota.

Recently, a new Shaoxing speedboat has been operating on the Xitang to Xiadianmiao Taozhuang route. It travels very quickly, and passengers are crowded. Yesterday, near Xiadianmiao, a bandit ship sailed head-on and fired a gun to force it to stop. Jiaxing

Rice Shop Raises Rice Prices and the County Punishes Them 185

Rice prices in Jiaxing have always been manipulated by rice merchants, so the prices sold are always more expensive than other ports. After social figures appealed to the party and government for relief, a joint party and government meeting was held five days ago, and members of the Rice Price Evaluation Committee were invited to participate. It was resolved that various rice prices would be appropriately reduced from the 6th to benefit the people. However, the agreed prices were still more expensive than those in Jiashan, Pinghu, Xiashi, and other places, so the citizens were not very satisfied. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the 6th, Yushui Rice Shop outside the North City of this port sold Dongmi to Yu Yongchang's Line Workshop for 17 yuan and 6 jiao (exceeding the resolution by 7 jiao), and Dajiao was still sold for 15 yuan (exceeding the resolution by 3 yuan). Someone held a statement and reported the matter to the party headquarters for investigation. It is learned that the party headquarters has decided to send a letter to the county for severe punishment of the case and to designate the funds collected from the fine to supplement the construction costs of the Seven Martyrs Memorial Pagoda and the Zhongshan Park construction to serve as a warning to others.

Educational Commissioners of the Seven Districts Appointed 186

Jiang Jingshuang, Director of the Jiaxing Education Bureau, determined that the autonomous region of this county has been decided to be seven districts, and in order to seek educational development and harmonious implementation, the current eight-district system will also be changed to seven districts. This has been approved by the Education Department and will be implemented from August 1st. The educational commissioners of each district have also been appointed: Zhao Taiqi for the first district, Shao Xiuzhang for the second district, Tao Bahong for the third district, Niu Jiechun for the fourth district, Ma Liuzi for the fifth district, Yuan Wen for the sixth district, and Yang Taoran for the seventh district. Their jurisdiction will be handled in accordance with the autonomous region.

Request to Increase Funds for Emergency Repair of Seawalls 187

The Hanghai Section Engineering Office of the Zhejiang Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau originally stipulated an annual emergency repair cost of 7,000 yuan. Now that emergency repairs are being carried out on dangerous seawalls, with thousands of workers being employed daily, the required funds are enormous. The provincial government, based on the handover of two kidnappers, Li Qinghu and Zhang Fuquan, by the Public Security Bureau, concluded the interrogation by the Fourth Section and escorted them to Qingbomen for execution by firing squad.

Hefei

Martial Law Declared for City Defense 190

Wei Lihuang, the commander of the Anhui North Garrison and the commander-in-chief of bandit suppression in the province, has now divided the province into seven bandit suppression zones. Hefei, Shouxian, Fengtai, Chaoxian, Hezhou, Dingyuan, Hanshan, Shucheng, Wuwei, Huaiyuan, Fengyang and other eleven counties are the second zone. Song Shike, commander of the Third Detachment and commander of the Hefei Defense, was appointed concurrently as the bandit suppression commander of the third zone. Commander Song, in order to prevent traitors, has appointed Cheng Yi, the commander of the First Regiment, as the chief of the military and police inspection office. The inspection office has been established and is responsible for patrolling day and night, and martial law has been declared. From the 5th, pedestrians are not allowed to pass after 11:00 PM without lights. The city is divided into five zones, and military police are ordered to check household registrations in sections.

Letter

Letter from Jingjiang County Public Security Bureau 191

We were surprised to read in the Jingjiang Communication column of your newspaper on July 31st that the county police team and the public security bureau had a conflict over a soil inspection, which is not in line with the facts. Upon investigation, County Chief Wang of our county secretly dispatched Captain Wang of the County Police Team to lead more than ten plainclothes officers in batches to the 8th District based on the report that a large amount of opium would be unloaded at the docks of the 6th, 7th, and 8th Districts. The officers dispatched to the 8th District did not have any official documents or symbols with them. When they arrived at the port, they were spotted by the public security bureau's patrol officers, who reported to Bureau Chief Chen of the bureau that two people wearing plainclothes and carrying box guns were at the Yidu Pier as if waiting for the ferry. Bureau Chief Chen went to investigate and found three people there. Upon questioning, they claimed to be officers of the police team. Because it was a time of martial law and there was no way to prove that they were officers, he had to temporarily disarm them. Later, Captain Wang arrived and provided proof for them, and Bureau Chief Chen immediately returned their weapons and sent police to assist in their work. During the inspection of passengers, a certain officer of the team had a conflict with the head of the security group of the port over the right of way. The head of the group's clothes were torn by the officer, and they were immediately brought to the Public Security Bureau. While they were arguing over the merits of the case, the officers of the 6th District had arrived and saw their colleagues arguing with others, and without asking the facts, they started arguing with Bureau Chief Chen, starting with insults and then with beatings. After Captain Wang stopped them, both sides reported to County Chief Wang, who punished the troublemaking group police separately. There was no incident of soil conflict as reported in your newspaper. It is assumed that your newspaper's interviewer did not get the true facts of the matter when interviewing. Fearing that the rumors would be inaccurate, we dare to send you this letter detailing the situation and requesting that it be published in the Letters section for correction. We eagerly await your response. Jingjiang County Public Security Bureau, Water Police Security Group, Third Detachment, August 7th.

Educational News

Important News

Overview of Education in Britain and America 192

According to the survey of the International Bureau of Education in Geneva, the recent situation of education in Britain and the United States is summarized below:

Schools in Various Regions of Wales, UK 193

According to the recent statistics report of the British Ministry of Education, the number of students in elementary schools in various places in Wales last year was decreasing, while the number of students in secondary schools increased by 1,563. The number of students in elementary schools decreased by 5,482. The reason for the decrease in the number of students in elementary schools is that most unemployed labor families have moved to other places, and the national birth rate has decreased by more than 33% in the past ten years. With the decrease in the number of students, the number of students in each class has also decreased. The largest number of classes had 16 classes, each with more than 60 students. The next largest number had more than 400 classes, each with 50 students. The ratio of students to teachers is 38 teachers for every 1,000 elementary school students, of which 24 have been registered and licensed as teachers by local educational institutions, 12 have not gone through this procedure, and the remaining 2 are supplementary teachers. The number of secondary school students in 1928 totaled 36,804, of which 19,277 were males and 17,527 were females. According to the survey last year, the total number had increased to 38,367, of which 20,145 were males and more than 18,000 were females, an increase of 868 males and 695 females, for a total increase of 1,563 male and female students. The ratio of students to the population is 14 secondary school students per 1,000 people. The average cost of education is 23 pounds, 9 shillings, and 6 pence per year for each secondary school student. The highest cost of living is 27 pounds and 7 shillings per year, and the lowest cost of living is only 19 pounds and 14 shillings.

Educational Expenses in New York and Chicago 194

The total number of primary and secondary school students in Chicago, USA, is now more than 464,800, and the total number of primary and secondary school students in New York City is now more than 1,018,800. According to the proportional number, the ratio should be 100 to 46, but the actual school expenses of the two cities are 100 to 34. The total annual salary of primary and secondary school teachers in New York is more than US$106 million, while the annual salary in Chicago is only more than US$36.7 million. This is because the salaries of teachers in the two cities are different, and the living standards in the two places are also different.

Budget and Recurring Expenses of Private New York University 195

The total budget for private New York University this year is US$7,530,000, an increase of more than US$950,000 compared to last year, and an increase of 18 times compared to 1911. It is found that the school's expenses in that year were 420,000 yuan, which increased to 820,000 yuan in 1916, 1.78 million yuan in 1920, and 3.05 million yuan in 1925. This is the approximate increase in expenses in the past 20 years. Among them, the salaries of faculty and staff were 3.58 million yuan last year, and the new budget has increased to 4.02 million yuan. The expenses for scientific instruments and utensils and expenses are 500,000 yuan. The expenses for purchasing and binding books in the library are 75,000 yuan. The management and repair of school buildings are 900,000 yuan. The distribution of expenses is as follows: 1.8 million yuan for the College of Arts and Sciences, 1.02 million yuan for the College of Commerce, 770,000 yuan for the College of Engineering and Science, 890,000 yuan for the College of Education, 500,000 yuan for the College of Medicine, 410,000 yuan for the College of Dentistry, 250,000 yuan for the College of Law, 250,000 yuan for the Graduate School, and 200,000 yuan for the Summer School.

US Federal Government Allocates Education Fees for American Red Indians 196

American newspapers reported that the American federal government's parliament has approved the case of education for the children of the Red Indians, who have struggled and improved their treatment over the years. Starting from July 1st of this year, the annual education fees for the children of the Red Indians will be increased by more than US$660,000 from the federal government. A standard will be formulated according to the minimum daily needs of each child's food and clothing specified by President Hoover, which is estimated to be US$0.378 per student per day for food and US$42.22 per student per year for clothing.

Schools' Receipts and Certificates Should Have Revenue Stamps Affixed 197

The Ministry of Education, upon approval from the Ministry of Finance, issued a circular to national, specialized, and higher education institutions, as well as to provincial and municipal education departments, stating that all kinds of money receipts and certificates of completion and transfer should uniformly bear revenue stamps. It was noted that the Ministry of Finance had previously requested that all schools affix revenue stamps to all kinds of money receipts, which was published in the Ministry's Gazette, Volume 2, No. 8, and circulated for compliance. Now, the Ministry of Finance has again advised: "It has been found that various schools still do not uniformly affix revenue stamps to all kinds of money receipts as required. Furthermore, specialized schools and higher institutions' certificates of completion and transfer should each bear a revenue stamp of one dime, while middle schools and schools of equal standing should each bear a revenue stamp of four cents, as stipulated in the regulations. Many schools have not complied, resulting not only in losses to the national treasury but also hindering the inculcation of revenue stamp awareness and the development of widespread habits. It is requested that all schools be instructed to uniformly affix revenue stamps to all kinds of receipts and certificates as per regulations, to maintain the national treasury and comply with the law in its entirety." The Ministry, in addition to forwarding copies, urgently orders that the aforementioned departments instruct all schools to comply uniformly.

The Calamity of the Qixia Rural Normal School 198

The Nanjing Middle School's Qixia Mountain Rural Normal School is one of the most renowned rural experimental normal schools in the country. The school's director, Huang Zhifu, has painstakingly managed it for years, achieving its current success. During this summer vacation, aside from Huang and a few staff members remaining at the school, there were also three students from distant places who stayed and did not return home. Unexpectedly, this has caused a major upheaval. Several days ago, the Capital Garrison Headquarters notified the Ministry of Education, stating that according to detective reports, students from several schools in the capital, including certain ones, were found to have communist elements within them, and requested that the affiliated schools be instructed to pay attention. The Qixia Rural Normal School was also on the list of schools to be watched. After receiving the report, the Ministry of Education informed Nanjing Middle School Principal Zhang Tong. Upon hearing this, Zhang made a mountain out of a molehill. In addition to immediately hiring Wu as the new director of the rural normal school, he also sent three staff members to Qixia on the 5th to take over from the rural normal school director, Huang. Huang had just received his renewal contract for the position of rural normal school director for the next academic year the day before. The sudden takeover was only permitted on the condition that it would be transferred after the handover was completed. Huang himself deeply knew that the teachers, staff, and students in the school were pure in their words and actions and that, apart from focusing on rural education research, they had never participated in external affairs. Now, encountering this unexpected blow, he was deeply shocked and bewildered. Therefore, yesterday morning (the 7th), he went to the Ministry of Education to meet with Vice Minister Zhu to inquire about the truth of the matter. It was reported that the Capital Garrison Headquarters' report was of a general nature and not specifically targeted at the Qixia Rural Normal School. Its intention was merely to hope that all schools would take precautions against possible troubles and did not carry any special meaning. The Ministry's notification to Principal Zhang was only to ask him to pay attention, not to instruct him to remove Director Huang. Moreover, the Ministry of Education has always highly praised Huang's performance in running the school over the years and would never use vague rumors to incriminate someone and endanger the protection of human rights in the education field. It was also heard that Zhang has rehired Huang as the director of the normal science department in the high school, but Huang believes that rural education is his lifelong career and hopes that the Qixia Rural Normal School will not be affected by his personal departure in the promotion of the rural normal school cause.

Sports

Public Tennis Doubles Final at 4 PM Today 203

Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia vs. Qiu Feihai and Jiang Daozhang

丨Yesterday's Semifinals丨 Kata and Yu Liu Fail. The Shanghai Chinese Open Tennis Doubles Semifinals were held at the Chinese Tennis Court yesterday afternoon starting at 2:30 PM. The audience was very enthusiastic and spirited. As a result, the Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia team and the Qiu Feihai and Jiang Daozhang team won the right to compete in the final. The Lin-Zheng team defeated the Canavero and Tafels team by scores of 2-6, 6-4, and 6-4. The Qiu-Jiang team defeated the Yu Tianguang and Liu Keng team by scores of 6-2, 7-5, and 6-3. The details are as follows:

(1) Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia 2-6, 6-4, 6-4 Defeat Canavero and Tafels 204

The match between Lin-Zheng and Kata started at 2:30 PM. Lin Baohua arrived late and rushed onto the court, appearing quite flustered. The first set was lackluster and uneventful. Kata won easily with a score of 6-2. From then on, both sides fought harder and the competition became very intense, completely different from the first set. Zheng Zhaojia showed great skill and Lin Baohua's solid technique made it difficult for Kata to cope, exhausting them. As a result, they won three sets in a row and achieved the final victory. The referee was Xu Zhendong.

First Set... 2-6 205

Both sides were negligent at the start of the match, and there were no highlights. However, Canavero remained steady as always and did not diminish his performance. Lin Baohua served and attacked, but the opponent's counterattack was effective, winning the first game and boosting their morale slightly. Lin-Zheng suffered repeated setbacks and made many mistakes, losing four games in a row. They then quickly tried to catch up and scored two more games. However, bad luck struck, and they were unable to do as they wished. As a result, Canavero won the set with a score of 6-2. The referee made many oversights in this set. Tafels often jumped his foot when serving, gaining a lot of advantage, and only changed slightly after being warned by the referee.

Second Set... 6-4 206

The situation became more intense starting from the second set. Lin-Zheng had good coordination and proper positioning, and were able to cope with ease. However, the opponent's strength did not seem to slacken. The first game victory still belonged to Kata. Subsequently, Tafels made great use of his wonderful shots. Although Lin Baohua smashed hard, all the shots were intercepted by Tafels. The ball was like cannon fire, making for a spectacular back-and-forth. Lin-Zheng won two consecutive games, and the opponent also scored a game, making the score 2-2. It then went to 3-3, with both sides holding their ground. Brilliant shots were frequently seen, eliciting cheers from the audience. The young hero Zheng Zhaojia repeatedly showed off his skills, cooperating effectively with his teacher Lin Baohua. Using either interceptions or smashes, he soon took the lead with a score of 5-2, creating a superior situation and winning this set with a score of 6-4.

Third Set... 6-4 207

In this set, the competition between the two sides became more intense, with strict defenses and very few mistakes. The situation was tense and each side had its own achievements. Kata took the lead and repeatedly gained the upper hand. However, after the score was 2-2, Lin-Zheng suddenly took the lead with a score of 3-2. Kata did not fall behind and closely followed. After the score was 4-4, it was Lin Baohua's turn to serve, and he continuously landed four heavy, cannonball-like serves. The opponent was unable to resist, and they took the lead again with a score of 5-4. As a result, their momentum surged. At this critical moment, they were unwilling to let go, like hungry tigers pouncing on sheep, brave and extraordinary. In a few rounds, they won another game and won the third set with a score of 6-4.

Fourth Set... 6-4 208

After a short break after the three sets, they lined up and fought again. Lin-Zheng, having taken the lead with a score of 2-1, would have achieved a complete victory if they had won one more set. However, Kata had to boost their spirits and fight to the death in this serious situation, hoping to reverse the situation and reach the fifth set final. Since the start of the battle, after Lin-Zheng had won the first game, the opponent used sharp interceptions to break Lin-Zheng's smashes, losing three consecutive games and taking the lead with a score of 3-1. Before long, it became 4-2, and Kata's momentum was fierce, with Lin-Zheng in a precarious situation. Then, they shook off their spirits and worked hard. Zheng Zhaojia served with great force, winning all four serves, and the situation slightly changed. The battle became more intense. Lin-Zheng continued to work hard and finally won again with a score of 6-4, securing the right to advance to the final.

Today's Open Tennis Doubles Champions 209

(Right) Lin Baohua (Left) Zheng Zhaojia

(Right) Qiu Feihai (Left) Jiang Daozhang

(2) Qiu Feihai and Jiang Daozhang 6-2, 7-5, 6-3 Defeat Yu Tianguang and Liu Keng 210

The match between Qiu-Jiang and Yu-Liu started at 5 PM. Yu-Liu was in a bad situation in the first set and was almost entirely controlled by Qiu-Jiang. Yu-Liu changed their strategy in the second set, guarding the side of the net and responding appropriately. The audience's spirits were greatly boosted at this point. Although they were ultimately defeated by Qiu-Jiang, it was indeed the most impressive set of the three. Yu-Liu still showed considerable effort in the third set, but because they were tightly pressed by Qiu-Jiang, they could not move as freely as in the second set. Therefore, they still suffered defeat. Qiu-Jiang won the right to compete in the final with a score of three to zero. The referee was Hu Lusheng.

First Set... 6-2 211

At the start of the match, the veteran Qiu-Jiang was indeed extraordinary, playing with great verve. Yu-Liu looked flustered and made a big mess. Therefore, they lost the first four games without showing any sign of vitality. Fortunately, Yu-Liu each won a game when it was their turn to serve, allowing them to avoid a complete defeat and lose with a score of two to six.

Second Set... 7-5 212

Seeing that the skill levels of the two teams were significantly different, the audience's interest greatly decreased, and they entered a state of semi-sleep. Then, the young heroes Yu-Liu made a timely effort to strive for success, which was due to the change in strategy. At this time, the two were stationed at the side of the net, intercepting at every opportunity. The two veterans initially did not want to be too harsh, intending to use their losses to encourage the younger generation. Seeing the opponent's agile skills, they were also surprised. Looking back at the scoreboard, Yu-Liu had already taken the lead with a score of three to zero. Subsequently, Qiu-Jiang changed their tactics, and the situation immediately reversed. Before long, they took the lead with a score of five to three. Yu-Liu made a comeback, using the net to win and creating a five-to-five tie. However, they failed at the last moment, and Zheng-Jiang won with a score of seven to five.

Third Set... 6-3 213

The atmosphere in the third set was tense, the situation was serious, and the future was bright for the two young tennis players. They took the lead in every attack, and the veteran Qiu-Jiang, although victory was in their grasp, faced them with full concentration and did not slack off. Yu-Liu initially took the lead with a score of one to zero. Qiu-Jiang tied it. Yu-Liu then took the lead twice with scores of two to one and three to two. After three to three, Qiu-Jiang fully demonstrated their abilities and soon won with a score of six to two. As a result, Qiu-Jiang won the right to compete in the final with a score of three to zero.

Local News

Wang Zhending Met Shighemitsu Yesterday 225

Japan and other countries did not protest the Hunan Incident

They only verbally asked for an explanation

Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting met with Japanese Acting Minister Shighemitsu yesterday morning at the Foreign Affairs Discussion Meeting for about an hour and a half before Shighemitsu departed. Later, Finnish Chargé d'Affaires Wei Meiji visited to discuss the rescue of missionaries in Jiangxi Province. Wang told reporters yesterday that Shighemitsu discussed various incidents during his visit. Japan and other countries have not formally protested to the Foreign Ministry about the Changsha incident. They only verbally asked for an explanation. The government has not yet received detailed reports, so it has not been able to give any feedback to various countries. Regarding the Sino-Japanese Ningbo case, the Japanese side's claimed losses are too high and there is not enough evidence, so the investigation is still ongoing.

Returning of the French Municipal Council Note 226

Delivered Directly to the French Legation in Beijing by the Foreign Ministry

Not Forwarded by the Shanghai Office

Regarding the issue of reclaiming the French Concession's Municipal Council, the Foreign Ministry's Shanghai office denied yesterday that a note had been sent to the French Consul in Shanghai for forwarding to the French Ambassador. When reporters met with Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting yesterday, they inquired about this matter. Wang said that the note to French Ambassador Wei Lide regarding the reclaiming of the French Municipal Council was sent directly to the French Legation in Beijing by the Foreign Ministry three or four days ago for forwarding to Beiping, without needing to be forwarded by the Shanghai office.

Victory Telegram Received by the Garrison Headquarters 227

A telegram from Liuhe on the 9th stated: "Commander Xiong, Shanghai, our anti-rebellion forces on the Jinpu Railway line are working hard to kill the enemy. The enemy's corpses are strewn about north and south of Wenshui. The number of prisoners and spoils of war is evident in the previous telegrams. Since the right-wing army captured Tai'an at the hour of 5 PM on the day of Yu, they have continued to pursue. Over the past two days, all left, central, and right routes have advanced separately. After retreating from Tai'an, the enemy has fled to Jinan along the railway line, abandoning military supplies and equipment beyond count. Our right-wing army has approached Jinan. Our central army, after defeating the enemy at Gushan and Taoshan north of Feicheng, will also join forces at Jinan. The left-wing is also approaching its rear via Pingyin and Changqing. Looking at the progress of the armies in the past two days, Jinan can be taken at any moment, and the enemy's retreat on the Jiaoji Railway has been cut off. The main force is blocking its front, and the long river is blocking its rear. The enemy forces entering Shandong have become turtles in a jar, and the time to annihilate them is imminent. A telegram is sent to announce the victory. General Commander's Train Staff Office."

Hunanese in Shanghai Launch a Campaign to Save Hunan 228

Fourteen Measures Decided at Yesterday's Meeting

Hunanese in Shanghai Hosted the Press Yesterday

Hunanese in Shanghai held a meeting at the Great China Hotel yesterday afternoon at 1 PM to discuss the Hunan incident. More than one hundred people attended. After two hours of discussion, fourteen measures were decided regarding the Hunan incident: (1) Request the authorities to quickly send elite troops to thoroughly suppress the bandit communists in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces. (2) Punish He Jian, the Hunan Chairman who abandoned his post, and the Provincial Party Committee and Provincial Government Committee, etc. (3) Reorganize the Party and government organizations. (4) Investigate the situation of the burning, killing, and looting in Changsha and the damages in Pingliu. (5) Request the authorities and compatriots across the country to raise huge sums of money to relieve the refugees. (6) Request the establishment of refugee shelters in various places. (7) Restore mass organizations to directly combat communism. (8) Organize Party member volunteer teams. (9) Organize people's anti-communist self-defense corps. (10) Each of the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi should station five divisions of troops to maintain law and order. (11) Resolutely restore political training in the army. (12) Eradicate corruption and build a clean government. (13) Publish anti-communist and save-Hunan publications, declarations, and circular telegrams. (14) Organize the Shanghai Hunanese Save-Hunan Association and send representatives to petition.

Moreover, yesterday afternoon at 3:30 PM, more than ten Hunanese refugee representatives, including Wei Jie Fu, hosted the press at the China Western Restaurant to report on the tragic situation of the communist bandits' disaster in Hunan. They criticized He Jian for his negligence in prevention beforehand and for abandoning his post without a fight after the incident. When Changsha had not yet fallen, he had told the people that he would vow to perish with the city and not to lightly believe in rumors and move their families. Unexpectedly, on the 27th, when the situation became tense, He's family was the first to flee, carrying as many as two hundred pieces of luggage. This threw Changsha into an irrecoverable abyss. How can this not be punished according to national law? It was said that there are about four thousand Hunanese refugees in Hankou, the most, and about several hundred in Shanghai. When they fled, they had nothing but the clothes on their backs and have been living with relatives and friends, experiencing much suffering. It is hoped that the media will provide assistance to promote the government to quickly find a way to thoroughly suppress the communist bandits in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces. The meeting adjourned at around 5 PM.

Ministry of Transportation Announces Process of Preparing Facsimile Telegraph 230

The facsimile telegraph service between China and Germany has been declared a success. Yesterday, the Ministry of Transportation announced the process of preparing for this service to the outside world, stating that facsimile telegraph is one of the modern new industries. It transmits original documents without using codes for sending and receiving, and the procedures are quite complex. The well-known systems include the Belrds system in France, the Karaluss system in Germany, and the Arcours system in the United Kingdom and the United States. Their effectiveness is gradually increasing. For example, even though airplanes in the air can communicate with the ground via wireless telegraphy, the noise of the engine often disturbs the sound waves of the messages, making them difficult to receive. Therefore, facsimile telegraph machines are used for communication. Moreover, Chinese characters are numerous, and telegraph transmission requires translation into codes before sending and receiving. With this machine, translation can be avoided, and the original text can be sent directly, and the meaning of the received telegram can be immediately understood. Now that the number of aircraft in China is increasing daily, air communication urgently needs to be prepared. Furthermore, this machine is most convenient for transmitting Chinese characters. Therefore, in order to develop China's telecommunications and facilitate public communication, the Ministry has requested the French Long-Distance Telephone Company and Siemens to transport facsimile telegraph machines to China for trial communication. The French company uses long-distance telephone lines to transmit facsimile telegrams, while Siemens uses one-way wireless reception to receive facsimile telegrams from Germany. They have already been installed and tested. Recently, the American Wireless Radio Victory Combined Company also intends to transport its machines to China for testing. The Ministry will determine the method after each company completes its testing, based on the results. The general situation of the two companies' trials is described below: (1) Last July, the French Long-Distance Telephone Company installed wired facsimile telegraph machines in the Beijing and Shanghai translation bureaus using long-distance telephone lines. The machine was invented by the French engineer裴灵氏. In the past, it was tested in post offices in the Pingjin and Northeast areas. The communication method uses contact transmission. After writing with ink, the sender needs to apply powder before transmitting, which is a tedious procedure, and the results are mediocre. Now, the machine has been replaced with a photocell, i.e., a neon gas lamp, so no powder is required for transmission, which is more perfect than the old machine. Since its trial use, the results have been good. (2) The Siemens machine is the 卡魯祿斯氏 type, produced by the German Telefunken Wireless Telegraph Company. It uses wireless communication to communicate with the Berlin 腦思 radio station. Preparation began in March of this year, using the remaining house of the 小營 instructor as a testing site. The company specially dispatched engineer 卢克思氏 from Germany to China to install it. Because the transmitting machine requires huge power to send over long distances, and the cost is too high, it is not easy to complete at once. Therefore, a receiving machine was first set up, using a directional antenna to receive reports from Germany. This machine was installed in June and began testing on June 26. At that time, a test telegram sent by colleagues from the embassy in Germany was received, taking only four and a half minutes. A few days later, three telegrams from Director 雙 of the Ministry from Germany were received, and the handwriting was very clear. The transmission of wireless facsimile telegrams between Europe and Asia was declared a success.

Social Affairs Bureau Asks Jianghai Customs to Strictly Investigate the Large-Scale Transport of Flour to the North 232

It is rumored that a certain foreign firm in this port has commissioned the Flour Exchange to purchase a large quantity of flour, which is about to be loaded onto ships and transported to the north. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, after receiving the report, believes that in this time of scarcity, flour is an essential commodity for regulating people's food supply. If grain is allowed to be supplied to the north, the people's food supply in this city will inevitably feel panic, and the market price may rise immediately. Moreover, the Ministry of Finance also has a prohibition on the export of rice and flour to the north. Therefore, it has sent a letter to the Jianghai Customs Supervision Office yesterday, asking it to strictly investigate to prevent smuggling.

Social Affairs Bureau Bans Rice Market "Net Settlement" 233

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau recently investigated that the shipping rice of the shipping companies has been sold in "net settlement" which is regarded as a disguised form of discount, and specially ordered Zhu Zixiang, chairman of the Rice Merchants Association, to ban it. The order is as follows: It is hereby ordered to investigate the matter. Previously, each rice shop in Nanshi pledged and was guaranteed by the chairman to apply for exemption from evaluation of the shipping rice. If the limited price is exceeded, heavy penalties will be imposed. The Bureau took into consideration the merchants' difficulties and temporarily approved it, and ordered the chairman to secretly investigate and report at any time, otherwise the penalty would be doubled. It is now found that the opening price of the shipping rice has reached 21 yuan, and commissions are posted outside the "net settlement" which is a disguised form of discount. The chairman's failure to prohibit it is inappropriate and should have been punished immediately, but he is given another pardon. The industry should be notified that there should be no more "net settlement" and other matters. If there is another violation, punishment will be imposed. It is also found that the rice market in Nanshi has recently been manipulated. If immediate correction is not made, the Bureau will have to take corresponding measures to prevent abuses and maintain the people's food supply. You are hereby informed.

Municipal People's Congress Conducts Investigation of Grain Work 234

Each Committee Member is Responsible for Conducting the Investigation

Recently, the arrival of foreign rice has been smooth, and the Rice Price Adjustment Committee has tried to transport and sell ordinary rice. As a result, the rice price has been maintained in its current state and has not seen a rise. However, although there are many arrivals, there is still a severe shortage of spot goods on the market, and the rice price has not been able to decline. This is indeed because someone is hoarding in the middle. After receiving reports from members of the Rice and Grain Special Committee of the Municipal People's Joint Association, the association has specially formulated several investigation methods and requested each member to be responsible for conducting them: (1) Investigate and advise rice stores along all roads to hang up rice and grain price signs, publicly displaying the prices of various rice varieties every day, and not to secretly mix in inferior goods or deduct the quantity; (2) Secretly investigate rice merchants hoarding rice and grain and privately mortgaging current funds to silver and money industries, waiting for the price to sell; (3) Secretly investigate rice merchants controlling rice and grain sources and manipulating rice prices; (4) Investigate rice merchants speculating and competing, buying and selling empty, and raising rice prices.

Pudong Cotton Expected to Have a Bumper Harvest 240

Cotton crops account for 70% of the farmland in the Pudong area of Shanghai. There were slightly too many rainy days after planting this year, and only two or three rainy days during the moldy rain season. The weather cleared up quickly, and weeds in the fields could be weeded in time. The temperature was very high, and the cotton seedlings grew very quickly. According to the records of the Zhoupu Jiangsu Provincial Cotton 南汇 Branch Farm, the average daily growth of cotton plants in July was 1.8CM. The cotton fields were slightly damaged by the two typhoons on July 14 and 27 and 28, but there was no major problem. Recently, the buds on the cotton plants have been growing vigorously, and the green bells are accumulating. They can be spun into floss in mid-August. If the weather does not change unexpectedly after autumn, it is predicted that a bumper harvest of 150 jin per mu can be obtained.

New Equipment Added to Inland Water Plant 242

Building a New Filtration Pool

Adding Electric Pumps

Investment of 500,000 Yuan

Among the water industry institutions operating in the city, the water supply of the Inland Water Company is the largest. The highest daily water supply in previous years was 18 million US gallons. The water plant is located on Bansongyuan Road in Nanshi, covering an area of 100 acres on the waterfront. The original water production equipment included two raw water pools, seven alum water pools, six slow sand filtration pools, seven rapid sand filtration pools, three clean water pools, and a pump room for inlet and outlet water. The scale was grand, but since its establishment 30 years ago, various equipment has inevitably become old and incomplete, affecting the water supply. This has long been criticized by the citizens of Nanshi. In recent years, under the supervision of the Municipal Public Works Bureau, the company has been determined to innovate, and the results have been remarkable. In the second half of the 18th year, the water pools and mechanical equipment were completely improved and six rapid filtration pools were added in accordance with the plan set by the Public Works Bureau. The filtration area is a total of 5,025 square feet, and the maximum water output is about 14 million Imperial gallons every 24 hours. The normal water output is about 12 million Imperial gallons. There are two concrete sedimentation pools with a total capacity of 1.8 million Imperial gallons. The longest flow time is about three and a half hours, and the shortest is about three hours. There is a water tower to store water for rinsing the sand and gravel in the rapid filtration pools, and its water tank capacity is 63,000 Imperial gallons. The layout of each part mostly uses the old pool site. It is planned to demolish the old slow sand pools Nos. 2 and 3 to rebuild the concrete sedimentation pools and transform the old raw water pool No. 2 into a new clean water pool. A new rapid filtration pool was rebuilt on its west end. Construction started on September 20 of last year and was originally scheduled to be completed in five months. However, it was extremely cold in winter and there was a lot of rain in spring. When the concrete pool was put into water for testing in early May of this year, the bottom of the old wall was leaking. The repairs took a lot of time. A reporter went to visit yesterday and saw that one of the concrete pools was already discharging water, and the sound of the clear stream pouring down was like a waterfall. It is said that this pool supplies 6 million gallons of water per day, accounting for about half of the total. Only because the remaining one has not yet been completed, the water cannot be diverted. The water in the new rapid filtration pool is still inevitably slightly muddy, but after chlorine gas disinfection, it is harmless to health. In the future, when all the old pools are completed, they will be shut down, and all the water from the concrete pool will be filtered through the new rapid filtration pool. The cleanliness of the water quality at that time will definitely be comparable to that of Zhabei. In addition, the new water pipes, water intake wells, and water intake and outlet engine rooms of the affiliated water pools are also under construction. The progress of the intake pipe can be buried. The river mud filled as soon as it was dug during the two recent typhoons, thus delaying the construction. The water intake well has been excavated. Both water intake and outlet machine rooms have been completed and are being installed. All the machinery is a new type of electric pump that can pump 48 million gallons of water every 24 hours. With this, it is really more than enough to cope with the current daily water consumption of about 12 million gallons. It seems that the 500,000 residents of Nanshi will soon be able to enjoy clean and abundant drinking water.

Warning to the Manager 243

The French business water and electricity strike has been difficult to resolve for a long time. According to the person in charge of the union, the strike was purely caused by the capital side. Recently, the sound of mediation of the strike seems to have the hope of being resolved. However, the conditions promised by the manager to the workers have not been able to give the workers satisfaction, and he has proposed to dismiss a large number of workers. How can the workers accept it? Looking at the above, the right and wrong of this strike cannot be shirked by the manager孟梭郎. Recently, the union will issue a written warning.

We will discuss it again when the time comes. Please check and acknowledge. The Chinese General Chamber of Commerce in Batavia, Executive Committee of the Chinese National Goods Maintenance Association, July 17, 19th year.

Petition from Brush and Ink Industry for Tax Exemption on Books and Documents 252

Letter from the Trade Association to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

The Brush and Ink Trade Association sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on August 6th, stating: "Respectfully, we note that the Ministry of Finance has issued instructions that brushes, inks, and paper are not solely limited to educational purposes and should be distinguished from purely educational materials. We believe that while schools may also teach Western learning, they invariably begin with Chinese. Since Chinese is the foundation, all citizens, whether farmers, laborers, merchants, students, or soldiers, begin their education by learning to read and write, using brushes and inks. Therefore, brushes and inks are essential for education. Fortunately, the government is promoting education, aiming to ensure that all 400 million people can read and write. Hence, it has exempted books related to the 5,000-year-old national essence from customs duties, intending to facilitate the free circulation of books nationwide. Books rely on text, and text relies on brushes and inks. Brushes and inks are indeed essential educational supplies. Currently, the promotion of domestic goods includes brushes and inks, and the revitalization of industry also encompasses them. Moreover, brushes and inks are used to explain the meaning of books and to copy them. Should their free circulation nationwide be impeded? Our association has repeatedly considered that the raw materials for books are paper. Paper is taxed at half the rate before it becomes a book, and books are tax-exempt. However, the raw materials needed for brushes and inks, such as wool, bamboo, weasel hair, rabbit skin, wooden boards, glue, borneol, and musk, are sourced from distant provinces and overseas. Within the country, they are subject to transit duties and consolidated taxes. At customs, they are subject to import and export duties, totaling over 20%. This is similar to the customs duties on paper, the raw material for books. While books are exempt from taxes, the raw materials for brushes and inks, which support education, should also be considered for exemption. Furthermore, after the materials are made into brushes and inks, their transport from Shanghai for export incurs significant customs duties, estimated at over 10% of their value. The double taxation has reached an extreme. Since 1927, the cost of brush and ink production, along with food and miscellaneous expenses, has doubled. Consequently, sales have been sluggish, with domestic and international sales totaling only around 500,000 yuan. The brush and ink business is declining daily. We believe that apart from public and private organizations and shops, schools are the primary consumers of brushes and inks. If the government could benefit students and alleviate the difficulties of merchants by exempting customs duties on brushes and inks, facilitating their unimpeded transport, not only would brush and ink merchants benefit, but the entire nation, which uses brushes and inks to study books and writing, would also be blessed. Our association estimates that brush and ink tax revenue, based on 10% of annual sales, amounts to about 50,000 yuan. Converted to customs taels, this is likely no more than 30,000 taels. The total annual customs revenue of Jianghai Customs is over 20 million taels. Exempting 30,000 taels for brushes and inks is like losing a hair from an ox or a grain from a granary. Therefore, we request that you consider the example of tax exemption for books and documents and exempt customs duties on brushes and inks, benefiting students and alleviating the difficulties of merchants. This is truly a matter of public convenience."

Dismissal of Road Employees Falsely Claiming Sick Leave 255

Yang Zicong's Desire for Comfort

The Traffic Director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways issued a notice to all employees yesterday morning, stating: "According to instructions from the Administration Bureau, which were relayed from the General Affairs Department, the Chief Medical Officer of the two railways, Xie Yingrui, reported that Gu Puquan, a physician at the Beizhan Clinic in Shanghai, had reported that Yang Zicong, an accountant, had visited the clinic on June 27th complaining of headache, fever, and loss of appetite. The physician diagnosed the condition, provided treatment, and granted two days of sick leave for rest. On July 1st, Yang requested an extension of three days. The physician determined that the illness had not fully resolved and approved the extension. However, on July 4th, when the leave expired, Yang again requested an extension. The physician found that the illness had fully recovered and denied the request. Yang then became agitated and left in anger. On July 7th, Yang sent a certificate from the accounting department stating that he was too ill to get out of bed and requesting a home visit from a physician. The physician immediately visited Yang's home and found him not only not ill but in good spirits. When asked why he required a home visit despite not being ill, Yang claimed to feel unwell only at night and requested another week of leave. The physician, assuming this might be true, asked Yang to visit the clinic for a certificate. On July 10th, the accounting department sent another notice stating that Yang was too ill to get out of bed and requesting a home visit. The physician immediately visited and found Yang physically and mentally healthy, with no signs of illness. When Yang requested another week of leave, the physician refused, stating that he was not ill and should be hospitalized if he felt unwell at night. Yang said he was ill because he wanted comfort. Since he needed hospitalization, why was he requesting leave? The physician firmly refused the request and returned. The physician reported that Yang, having been denied leave, reported for duty on July 11th. It is clear that Yang Zicong intentionally feigned illness to obtain leave and make things difficult for the physician. Article 5 of the temporary regulations for sick leave for employees of the two railways states that if an employee is unable to visit the railway clinic or hospital due to illness, a physician may visit the home to issue a certificate. Yang, being able to move freely, feigned illness and requested a home visit, violating these regulations. It is respectfully requested that the Director issue an appropriate punishment to deter others."

The report stated: "Accountant Yang Zicong repeatedly feigned illness to request leave, intentionally violating regulations and neglecting duties. If not severely punished, others may follow suit, undermining discipline and railway operations. The Ministry of Railways has ordered that Yang be dismissed as a warning to others." Therefore, it is ordered that the accounting department comply and that all employees adhere to regulations, refraining from requesting leave without reason to avoid investigation.

Overcharging of Refugees by Swire Shipping's Suiding Boat 267

Boat from Changsha to Hankou

A Charge of 900 Yuan Per Seat

The American Evening Post reports that the Swire Shipping Company's steamship Suiding departed Changsha as the city fell. Desperate to escape to Hankou, Changsha residents crowded onto the ship. The crew took the opportunity to overcharge passengers, demanding 300 yuan for a first-class cabin that normally costs 45 yuan from Changsha to Hankou. Similarly, they charged 900 yuan per seat in the captain's cabin and 200 yuan per seat in the crew's cabins. It is estimated that the 500 passengers paid at least 20,000 yuan in excessive fares. Most refugees emptied their pockets to pay, and when some begged to keep one yuan to buy food upon arrival in Hankou, the crew refused without pity. After arriving in Hankou, the ship left for an unknown destination. Its whereabouts have not been determined.

Butcher Turns to Butchering People

Motivated by Professional Jealousy

Butcher Zhu Ada and Wang Caibao had a long-standing feud due to competition in the same trade. Zhu was known for his violent temper and had often threatened Wang. Due to the summer heat and the cramped quarters of Wang's residence on Yuezhou Road, Wang moved outside to sleep on a mat in the alleyway. The previous night, Wang and his friend Zhu Shunbao were sleeping in the open air when, around 3:00 AM, Zhu Ada arrived with several accomplices, some carrying guns, others axes. At that time, the crescent moon and cool breeze were present, so Wang and Zhu were in deep slumber. Their dreams were shattered when Zhu Ada arrived and attacked them with axes. Wang was hit in the hands and feet, screaming in pain, and fell to the ground bleeding. Zhu Shunbao was terrified by the attack and threat and did not interfere. The attackers fled with their weapons. Nearby police, hearing reports from passersby, arrived and captured Zhu Ada. The injured Wang was taken to Tongren Hospital for treatment, and Zhu Ada was taken to the Harbin Police Station for detention. However, Zhu suddenly developed cholera, a serious condition, and the police sent him to the hospital. Yesterday morning, only the witness, Zhu Shunbao, was brought to the Special District Court. The police lawyer, Zhang Dayin, explained the cause of the conflict. Both the victim and the attacker were in the hospital, so the case was adjourned.
